Enclosed is a copy of the Agenda for the Board of Education meeting to be held on Wednesday,
May 23, 2018. The meeting will be held at CPS Loop Office, 42 West Madison Street, Garden Level, Board
Room. The Board Meeting will begin at 10:30 am.

Public Participation Guidelines are available on or by calling (773) 553-1600.

For the May 23, 2018 Board Meeting, advance registration to Speak and observe will be available
beginning Monday, May 21St at 10:30 am. and will close on Tuesday, May 22nd at 5:00 pm, or until all
slots filled. Advance registration during this period is available by the following methods:

Online: 
Phone: (773) 553-1600 .
In Person: 1 North Dearborn Street, Suite 950

The Public Participation segment of the meeting will begin immediately following the CEO Report
and proceed for no more than 60 registered speakers for the two hours.

The complete, final Agenda of Actions from the April 25, 2018 Board meeting is on our website:


Sincerely,


Estela G. Beltran
Secretary
